<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-RIGHT: 18pt">Dear AEI Fund 25 Limited Member:</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">This letter and the enclosed consent documents are provided to request your vote on operational matters concerning AEI Income &amp; Growth Fund 25 LLC, in which you have invested as a limited member. We refer to this investment as "Fund 25" or "the Fund" throughout these documents.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The enclosed Consent Form provides you with the opportunity to vote on four proposals:</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Proposal&#160;#1</u></font>. To instruct Fund 25 to begin liquidating itself. That means that it will begin selling its properties and terminating its existence once all property sales are completed. If this proposal is approved, you will begin receiving capital distributions as the property sales occur and your quarterly distributions from rental income will decline over time to zero when the last property is sold.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Proposal #2</u></font>. <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">As an alternative to Proposal #1</font>, to authorize Fund 25 to continue in operation for an additional 60 months from June 2018. If this proposal is approved, you will continue to receive quarterly distributions from Fund 25 operations, rather than capital distributions from the sale of its properties.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Proposal #3</u></font>. To amend Section 7.7 of the Fund's operating agreement to increase the price at which units may be repurchased under the Fund's unit repurchase plan from 80% of the estimated net asset value per unit to 95% of the estimated net asset value per unit. Under both the current operating agreement and the proposed amendment, the repurchase price is reduced by any distributions paid for the units for the quarter immediately preceding the date the units are repurchased.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Proposal #4</u></font>. To allow Fund 25 to sell joint venture interests that it currently owns in eight of its properties to other AEI Affiliated Funds. The remaining interests in these joint ventures are currently owned by other AEI Funds. <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">If any Fund 25 joint venture interests are sold to </font>affiliated Funds, the sales will be made <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">on an "as is, where is" basis and the price of each property will be based upon the property's fair market value as determined by an independent, third-party, commercial property appraiser</font>.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Prior to voting, you should carefully read the enclosed Consent Statement to understand the proposals and risks that may be associated with them. If you have any questions concerning this communication and vote request, please call AEI Investor Services, toll free, at 800-328-3519.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">Sincerely,</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div><br>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-RIGHT: 18pt">Managing Member</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center">CONSENT STATEMENT</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">We are providing this Consent Statement to all limited members of AEI Income &amp; Growth Fund&#160;25 LLC who are unit owners of record as of June 1, 2018. Through the enclosed Consent Form, we are soliciting your consent to the four proposals below:</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Proposal&#160;#1</u></font>. To instruct Fund 25 to begin liquidating itself by selling its properties and, thereafter, terminating its existence.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Proposal #2</u></font>. <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">As an alternative to Proposal #1</font>, to amend Section 11.3 of the operating agreement of Fund 25 to authorize it to continue in operation for an additional 60 months from June 2018, at which time another vote on this matter will be presented to the limited members.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Proposal #3</u></font>. To amend Section 7.7 of the operating agreement to increase the price at which units may be repurchased under the Fund's unit repurchase plan from 80% of the estimated net asset value per unit to 95% of the estimated net asset value per unit. Under both the current operating agreement and the proposed amendment, the repurchase price is reduced by any distributions paid for the units for the quarter immediately preceding the date the units are repurchased.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Proposal #4</u></font>. To allow Fund 25 to sell joint venture interests that it currently owns in eight of its properties to other AEI Affiliated Funds.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">To vote, you must return a properly signed Consent Form that is received by AEI Fund Management XXI, Inc. at 1300 Wells Fargo Place, 30 East 7th Street, St. Paul, Minnesota 55101, on or before 5:00&#160;PM, Central Time, on&#160;August 23, 2018.<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"> Please vote "FOR" only one of the first two proposals. Do not vote "FOR" both Proposal #1 and Proposal #2: they are mutually exclusive and cannot be implemented simultaneously.</font></div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">We encourage you to sign and return the enclosed Consent Form &#8211; your vote is important.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">We mailed this Consent Statement to you, as a limited member of Fund 25, on July 17, 2018.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center">QUESTIONS AND ANSWERS ABOUT THE PROPOSALS<font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><br>
</font> AND THE CONSENT SOLICITATION</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">BACKGROUND</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Q:</font><font id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 1px; WIDTH: 36pt; DISPLAY: inline-block; TEXT-INDENT: 0px">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">What are you asking me to do?</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z31f4b6ae91fb4b508a1e1462f6c3ffbb" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">We are asking you to vote by signing and returning the enclosed Consent Form:</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt">(1) on a proposal to instruct Fund 25 to begin liquidating itself by selling its properties and, thereafter, terminating its existence;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt">(2) on an alternative proposal to amend Section 11.3 of the operating agreement of Fund&#160;25 to authorize it to continue in operation for an additional 60 months from June 2018, at which time another vote on this matter will be presented to the limited members;</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt">(3) on a proposal to amend the unit repurchase plan of Fund 25 to increase the price at which units may be repurchased by the Fund to 95% of the estimated net asset value per unit, less any distributions paid for the units for the quarter immediately preceding the date the units are repurchased; and</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt">(4) on a proposal to allow Fund 25 to sell joint venture interests that it currently owns in eight of its properties to other AEI Affiliated Funds.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>Do not vote "FOR" both Proposal #1 and Proposal #2: they are mutually exclusive and cannot be implemented simultaneously</u></font>.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Q:</font><font id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 1px; WIDTH: 36pt; DISPLAY: inline-block; TEXT-INDENT: 0px">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Why are you asking for my vote?</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z60c60ccc11d24884a991c9a5db5069f2" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">Under Section 6.1 of the operating agreement of Fund 25, to sell all or substantially all of the Fund's properties, we are required to obtain the consent of a majority of the limited members by interest. We are asking for your vote on the first proposal to conform to the intent of the original offering of investment in this Fund.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt">We are asking for your vote on the second proposal because we believe Fund 25 provides a rate of current income that compares favorably to the income available from other investments. Many limited members may prefer to see a continuation of this current income as opposed to a liquidation of the Fund.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt">We are asking for your vote on the third proposal to provide the limited members with an opportunity to increase the price at which units may be repurchased under the Fund's unit repurchase plan from 80% of the estimated net asset value per unit to 95% of the estimated net asset value per unit. This will result in a repurchase price that more closely approximates what we believe to be the fair market value of the Fund's units.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt">We are asking for your vote on the fourth proposal because Fund 25 owns joint venture interests in eight properties with other AEI Affiliated Funds. Because most buyers of net leased real estate require ownership of an entire property, we believe that it would be difficult for Fund&#160;25 to sell these joint venture interests in the open real estate market. As a result, we are asking you to vote on a proposal to allow Fund 25 to sell its interests in these properties to other AEI Affiliated Funds. Although we believe that Section 6.6 of the Fund 25 operating agreement expressly contemplates such a sale to current joint-venture owners, Section 6.5(vii) also prohibits Fund 25 from selling properties to affiliated funds, therefore creating an ambiguity unless resolved. This vote would eliminate such ambiguity. In addition, this proposal would also allow Fund 25 to sell joint venture interests to any AEI Affiliated Fund, not just AEI Affiliated Funds that are current joint-venture owners.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt">&#160;</div>

<div id="DSPFPageBreakArea">
<div id="DSPFPageNumberArea" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font id="DSPFPageNumber" style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-STYLE: normal">-3-</font></div>

<div id="DSPFPageBreak">
<hr noshade="noshade">
</div>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Q:</font><font id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 1px; WIDTH: 36pt; DISPLAY: inline-block; TEXT-INDENT: 0px">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">May I vote "FOR" all proposals?</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="zf12f9bb8349a4097baaaa40b5e4fc6be" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>No</u></font>. Vote "FOR" only one of the first two proposals. Do not vote "FOR" Proposal #1 and "FOR" Proposal #2 at the same time. Proposal #1, if approved, will require the sale of the Fund's properties and the Fund's liquidation, while Proposal #2 will authorize the Fund to continue in operation. <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><u>If none of the proposals are approved</u></font>, the Fund will continue in operation without a specific time frame to liquidate and the increased unit repurchase price described in Proposal #3 will not take effect.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left">PROPOSAL #1 - LIQUIDATION</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z35de8d4f31634202b4d53bce2875c7cf" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Why is Proposal #1 being presented?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z4fd02826b94e4c17a7fc13c8c0ee202e" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">When Fund 25 was organized, the offering documents indicated the intent to sell the Fund's properties in 8 to 12 years following the completion of the property acquisition phase. In 2006, the Fund completed the investment of proceeds from the offering in properties. Under Section 6.1 of the operating agreement of Fund 25, the consent of a majority of the limited members by interest is required to sell all or substantially all of the Fund's assets.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="zd52b41961d04456f9bbe367172470f53" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">What will happen if limited members approve Proposal #1?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z12f7e9d77c854adeaaebd50f65a48688" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">The proposal, if approved, will instruct the Managing Members of Fund 25 to commence the orderly sale of the Fund's remaining 12 properties. We anticipate that the sales could be completed within 24 months. As sales are completed, Fund 25 would distribute the proceeds to the limited members of the Fund, less sale-related expenses, less the Managing Members interest in the proceeds, and less a reasonable operating reserve. Reserve funds would be distributed as part of a final dissolution of the Fund.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z190dc05c3f1e4650ba713f648aa552ff" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">If Proposal #1 is approved, how much cash might I receive?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="za8589b270ed14b6fa41ea07043da320f" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">We cannot know how much cash can be generated from the sale of the properties until the sales are actually completed. The value of the properties depends upon market conditions and the amount that the Fund would be able to distribute depends upon the terms of sale, as well as expenses incurred to complete each sale. Based upon current market conditions and capitalization rates for similarly situated properties, and our own internal analysis without independent appraisal, we estimate that approximately $30,933,000, or $773 per unit, would be available for distribution to the limited members. In making this estimate, we are assuming that Fund properties are sold in the normal course of business without extraordinary expense and that the properties continue to generate rental income during the sales period. It is likely that actual proceeds received will vary from this estimate and any variation could be material.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">Assuming the Fund was liquidated as of March 31, 2018 and that the estimated liquidation proceeds from the sale of properties were realized, and factoring in prior cash distributions received, an original investment in the Fund of $1,000, on September 11, 2003, would have received $1,510 in total distributions over the life of the investment.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Q:</font><font id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 1px; WIDTH: 36pt; DISPLAY: inline-block; TEXT-INDENT: 0px">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">What are the tax consequences of liquidation?</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z6eb0af4ad6a6482abc9c26aa5ebba41b" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">The sale of the properties and distribution of the liquidation proceeds may generate both ordinary income and capital gain or loss to the limited members for United States federal income tax purposes. Tax matters are complicated. Your tax consequences may depend upon your financial situation and whether you purchased your units in the original offering or the secondary market. Please consult your tax advisor to determine the tax consequences of liquidation to you.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>&#160;</div>

<table id="zf4da5e5a8bb240d1972b257496d3fe2a" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Do the Managing Members, or management of the Managing Members, have any interest in seeing Proposal #2 approved?</div>
</td>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="zd0cc8a26624e41b2acb79c7efdba497a" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">Potentially, yes. The Managing Members and their affiliates are reimbursed for the expenses incurred in operating Fund 25, including expenses of administering the Fund's properties. If the Fund is liquidated, these reimbursements would terminate. Although the reimbursements are at cost, they are calculated on the overall costs of the Managing Members and their affiliates in providing the services and, therefore, include a portion of the salaries and other compensation expenses of the Managing Members and their affiliates. <font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">On the other hand, if the Fund is liquidated, the Managing Members will receive a share of the liquidation proceeds.</font></div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left">PROPOSAL #3 &#8211; AMEND THE FUND'S UNIT REPURCHASE PLAN</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Q:</font><font id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 1px; WIDTH: 36pt; DISPLAY: inline-block; TEXT-INDENT: 0px">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">At what price does Fund 25 currently repurchase units?</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z8bda39342e114f4fb654f997afd0985f" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">Section 7.7 of the operating agreement of Fund 25 currently provides that unit repurchases by Fund 25 are made at a price equal to 80% of the estimated net asset value per unit, less any distributions paid for the units for the quarter immediately preceding the date the units are repurchased. At March 31, 2018, we estimated the net asset value per unit was $773.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z880c6e34041741518a57982ab4589d73" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Why do you want to increase the repurchase price?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z52598401c7334015954ccb95cdf71533" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">We believe that it is reasonable to provide the limited members with an opportunity to increase the price at which units are repurchased to a price that more closely approximates what we believe to be the fair market value of the Fund's units.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z463e76781d044608a89c6e082fd34b43" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Isn't a lower repurchase price under the unit repurchase plan favorable to the limited members who do not wish to sell their units?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z1e92e1c4399c4164bc352197857cc9c5" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">Yes. A lower repurchase price, if accepted by a tendering limited member, would be more favorable to limited members who remain in the Fund, than a higher price. However, at some point, a limited member may need liquidity and the higher price would result in that limited member receiving a price that the Managing Members believe is closer to the fair market value of the Fund's units.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Q:</font><font id="TRGRRTFtoHTMLTab" style="FONT-SIZE: 1px; WIDTH: 36pt; DISPLAY: inline-block; TEXT-INDENT: 0px">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Are there risks related to repurchases?</font></div>

<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">In addition to the possibility that repurchases may not be available, limited members should consider the following risks in connection with the Fund's unit repurchase plan:</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div>
<table id="z1edb0580db684fe5bd9fd6e8b2581421" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">The calculation of net asset value per unit is based upon estimates and assumptions and the knowledge and expertise of the Managing Members and Fund 25 may, eventually, realize values per unit that are more or less than the Fund's stated repurchase price;</div>
</td>

<div>
<table id="z18c7f6e6b19c4dcfa861618dbc30b098" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left">Limited members whose units are repurchased may incur a tax liability;</div>

<div>
<table id="z00383906cb584a34b80584b7975f17db" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 0.7pt">PROPOSAL #4 &#8211; SALE OF JOINT VENTURE INTERESTS TO OTHER AEI AFFILIATED FUNDS</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z16061b5d03674536ac7c968c91ba8260" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">What will happen if limited members approve Proposal #4?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z7c9f5258bf2c4733893f739bc4978ecd" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">The proposal, if approved, will allow Fund 25 to sell the joint venture interests it owns in eight properties to other AEI Affiliated Funds. The sales price for properties sold in this manner will be based upon an independent, third-party, commercial property appraisal.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z02eb9729a91942599d88d2b25a7e48de" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">If Proposal #4 is approved, what is the benefit to Fund 25?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z8aed2a525faf4a2c88fff24962cd4a8e" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">A sale of a joint venture interest in a property on the open real estate market could take many months, if not years. The sale to other Affiliated Funds could, however, can be completed in a relatively short time, resulting in the Fund receiving sale proceeds sooner. Furthermore, real estate brokerage commissions typically represent a seller-related expense and have historically ranged from 3% to 6% of a property's gross sale price. A sale to other Affiliated Funds will eliminate the expense of brokerage commissions, thereby potentially resulting in higher net sales proceeds to the Fund.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="zb45b5c8ed3e8469c9260ef1047b22a35" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">What if Proposal #4 is not approved</font>?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="zc7925964dcfb4be596fe99d04d7068cb" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">If the proposal to sell the Fund's properties to other Affiliated Funds is not approved, then Fund&#160;25 will attempt to sell the joint venture interests in the eight properties in the open real estate market. If the interests cannot be sold in timely fashion, the final liquidation of the Fund may be delayed.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left">THE CONSENT SOLICITATION PROCESS</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="zefff6d6410a242de897f987b396e38e5" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">What vote is required to approve the proposals?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z98c731df6cb047ef90b2dac8280b4b8f" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">The affirmative vote of a majority of the units of limited member interest in Fund 25 is required to approve a proposal.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="za6424e7c0e084f509676fdeb8c1f950a" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Am I required to vote on these proposals</font>?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z3d9a89ab30684e68925d84dafd84ca01" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">A:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif">No, you are not required to vote. However, not voting would have the effect of a vote against the proposals. If Proposal #1 to liquidate is not approved by limited members holding a majority of the outstanding units, then Fund 25 will continue in operation until the limited members vote to authorize the sale of all of the Fund's properties or December 31, 2053. If Proposal #3 is not approved by a majority of the units held by limited members, Fund 25 will continue to offer a unit repurchase price equal to 80% of the estimated net asset value per unit, less any distributions paid for the units for the quarter immediately preceding the date the units are repurchased. If Proposal #4 is not approved by limited members holding a majority of the outstanding units, Fund 25 will not sell any joint venture interests in properties to other AEI Affiliated Funds.</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; TEXT-INDENT: -36pt">VOTING PROCEDURES</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 6pt; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table id="z9c3cd4d0fc7c4fb695b5a0d37b0b390c" class="DSPFListTable" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 100%" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; WIDTH: 36pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Q:</td>
<td style="WIDTH: auto; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">How do I vote?</div>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The following summarizes the proposals being presented to the limited members of Fund&#160;25. You should read this entire Consent Statement to fully understand the proposals.</div>

Authorization to liquidate is required in accordance with Section 6.1 of the operating agreement prior to the sale of all or substantially all of the assets of the Fund.</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: center">BACKGROUND OF THE FUND</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">Fund 25</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">AEI Income &amp; Growth Fund 25 is a Delaware limited liability company organized in 2002. From May 13, 2003 through May 12, 2005, the Fund raised $42.43 million through a public offering of its units. The net proceeds from the offering were used to purchase, without mortgage debt, commercial real estate occupied by tenants under net leases. Fund 25 initially purchased fifteen properties, including partial interests in eight of these properties. The prospectus by which the units were originally offered indicated that properties would be sold from time to time and the cash proceeds invested in similar net leased properties.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">Although Fund 25 has not commenced the sale of properties in final liquidation, the Fund has sold properties and reinvested the majority of the proceeds in similar net leased properties. In all cases, the Fund distributed enough cash for limited members to pay the taxes generated by any income or gain recognized by them on sale of such properties.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; TEXT-ALIGN: justify">Properties</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">As of March 31, 2018, Fund 25 held interests in twelve properties. It also held net cash reserves of approximately $5,183,000. Eleven of the properties are subject to net leases under which the tenant pays substantially all of the property operating costs. The tenants in these properties are current with their rental payments and the properties are fully occupied. The other property is currently partially vacant as discussed below.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The Company owns a 60% interest in the Sports Authority store in Wichita, Kansas. On March&#160;2, 2016, the tenant, TSA Stores, Inc., and its parent company, The Sports Authority, Inc., the guarantor of the lease, filed for Chapter 11 bankruptcy reorganization. In June 2016, the tenant filed a motion with the bankruptcy court to reject the lease for this store effective June&#160;30, 2016, at which time the tenant returned possession of the property to the owners. As of March&#160;31, 2018, the tenant owed $29,049 of past due rent, which was not accrued for financial reporting purposes. The owners listed the property for lease with a real estate broker in the Wichita area. While the property is vacant, the Company is responsible for its 60% share of real estate taxes and other costs associated with maintaining the property.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">On September 21, 2017, the Company entered into a lease agreement with a primary term of 10&#160;years with Biomat USA, Inc. ("Biomat") as a replacement tenant for 28% of the square footage of the property. The tenant will operate a Biomat USA Plasma Center in the space. The Company's 60% share of annual rent is $55,607 and is expected to commence on June&#160;18, 2018. Biomat has agreed to pay for the costs to divide the building into two separate spaces, the costs of tenant improvements to remodel the Biomat space and 28% of the cost to replace the roof. The Company will be responsible for paying its 60% share of the remaining cost to replace the roof, which is expected to be approximately $170,000. At December 31, 2017, the Company accrued its 60% share of lease commissions due to real estate brokers totaling $81,440 that were owed as part of the lease transaction. This amount was capitalized and will be amortized over the term of the lease. The Company is continuing to pursue additional tenants for the remaining space.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div id="DSPFPageBreakArea" style="MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; MARGIN-TOP: 10pt; CLEAR: both">
<div id="DSPFPageNumberArea" style="TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font id="DSPFPageNumber" style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-WEIGHT: normal; FONT-STYLE: normal">-10-</font></div>

<div id="DSPFPageBreak" style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
<hr style="BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0px; HEIGHT: 2px; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0px; WIDTH: 100%; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0px; COLOR: #000000; CLEAR: both; MARGIN: 4px 0px; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0px; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #000000" noshade="noshade">
</div>
</div>

<div><br>
